
1a1(ka): / s+dzogs pa chen po nang zhung snyan rgyud kyi brgyud pa'i bla ma'i rnam thar bzhugs so// //

2b1(ka): phyag 'tshal lo// gang gi mtshan tsam rna bar this pas kyang / 'khor ba'i 'jigs 'phrog ngan 'gro'i gdung sel ba/ de phyir khyed kyi yon tan rgya mtsho las/ chu cigs tsam

2b4(ka): dkyil 'khor la 'jug pa la/ me ri zhi khro'i cho ga'i gzhung bsrang / nang dbang gi rim pas gang zag gi rgyud byin gyis brlabs/ gsang ba dbang gcig rgyud brta thabs mtshen pa'i

3a1(ka): mkhas kbyab ste/ nam mtha' hi kun la byab csi blos gnal znhing dpag pa dka' zhes 'o// des khyab cad nid kyis byab cing rgya che ste/ 'jig rten gyi thams 
3a2(ka): byang ba ma kyis maM khyab ste brangs mang zhe 'o// nye grangs mang bad bzhain du/ bzlud kyi sems can byang ba ma gyig ma khyab ste/ yo zhes spyan gyis gzigs pa'i sems can / 
3a3(ka): ni/ ci snyed pa'i rdul bas grangs mang bas zhes so// de mang ba bzhin du sems can gyi las kyang grangs mang ste/ sems can gyi las kyang bsam gyis mi khyab ste grangs mang zhes so// 
3a4(ka): 'dul zhing snod kyi 'jig rten rgya che/ gdul bya bcud kyi sems can grangs mang ba de bzhin du / 'dul byed bder gshegs kyis gsungs pa'i bon kyang bsam gyis mi khyab ste/ ston 
3a5(ka): pa'i bka' yang bsam gyis mi khyab ste grangs mango'o// zhes gsungs o// ston pas gsungs pa'i bon de la gnyis/ son gyi shra gang la 'jug pa dang / skabs don gyi bon ngos bzang

3b4(ka): gshegs bstan pa'i brjod bya'o// gnyis pa sgra don ni/ ston pas gsungs pa 'khor rnams kyi snyan du bon pas bon zhes bya'o// gsum pa dbye ba mchan tho bas byas pa'i dad rgyas

4a1(ka): / la tham khadkyin o/ gdma'gtsam khad kyi megdng ldra ba gsungs pa'dis bshad bya kho chos hyo cob kbya d nicon gyi re tcon'o / 
4a2(ka): bzung pa d'o znas/ gnyis pa 'chad mcan ston pa'i byon tshul la yang gnyis te/ ran rgyud mu chags du rgyud pa dang / nye rgyud tsig bbs du rgyud pa'i// dng por rgyud la yang 
4a3(ka): gnyis te/ rgyal ba dgongs pa'i rgyud pa dang / grub tsob snyan khung gi rgyud pa'o// dang po na/ gzer bu las/ dgongs pa'i thags rgyud ces pa la/ dgu ni y nyid ston pa dang thugs rje' /

4a6(ka): nyid khyab badal chen po' nin khams zhes bya ba/ rgyu rkyen lasam bskye/ snod bcudg du m chags/ mdog khbyebs du mgrub/ btha' dbung phyogs btsams du mi gnas pa/ 
4b1(ka): dbyings chen 'byams yas chen po'i klong na/ gnyis pa ston pa ni/ bdag med kyi kun tu bzang po/ 'khor 'das gang gis kyang mthas ma rig/ sangs rgyas sems can gnyis su

4b3(ka): kun gzhi ka dag chen po'i gnas nas/ rig pa rang shar gyi ston pas/ sems dang blo yid kyi 'khor la/ thugs rjes byin rlabs kyis skyob par byed pa ste/ sems kyi gnad drug las//

4b6(ka): // / gnyis pa thugs rje'i ston pa la gsum ste/ gnas dang / ston pa dang / dgongs pa'i rgyud tshul lo// dang po gnas ni/ mi g.yo mchan yig lung las// khyab bdal dbyings 
5a1(ka): kyi 'og min na/ zhes pa/ 'og men 'da' ba med pa'i po brang zhes bya ba/ s rdon brag med pa/ tsho 'brul 'od kyi gnal yas chang / ye shes kyi rang snang las grub

1a2(ta): / s+dzogs pa chen po nang zhung snyan rgyud las lta ba spyi gcod kyi mnyam bzhag sgom pa'i lag len bzhugs so// // / 
1a3(ta): bsgo hgo ghg g sgo gohgo go hgo sgo hgo khgo khog khgo khg gokhgoh gozhgo sgo hgro khgo khgro 'hgro khogo khgo khgo'ghg ghg hgo/ 
1b1(ta): +o// bnor mz hor rogs tom r sgon lbog'bako/ btag bhag ab kyi ggo ram gte la/ gba ggnon las
1b2(ta): la 'khred pa'i phyir/ rgyal ba dgongs rgyud dgu'i thugs kyi bcud/ gang zag nyi shu rtsa bzhi' man ngag dril ba/ mnyam bzhag sgom pa'i lag len bstan pa ni/ 
1b3(ta): brgyud pa bzhi dang ldan pa'i bla ma yis/ dad brtson shes rab snying rje ldan/ lha dang bla ma spyi boar bkur/ khong yangs kha dam zungs thub cing / blo brtyan mi 'gyur masang 
1b4(ta): ge' bu/ snod dang ldan pa'i slob bu la/ thugs bcud gdams ngag s+dzogs par bstan/ dben pa'i gnas su mthun rkyen 'dzoms par bya/ 'byung ba'i cha dang zas kyi / 
1b5(ta): bsila drod snyoms/ phyi nang 'grul bskyung bsam gtan cher ma song / sngon 'gro phyi nang yul dang zhes pa sbyang / dang po snang ba yul la sbyang pa ni/ mi lus thob par dka' 
2a1(ta): / g'don pa ba / tshb bod mi g na n don pa 'ldzog/ dl khyor b rtogs par 'tsobrgyau la ba g/ 'jig ton 'brul n gru b 'di'
2a2(ta): bslu bar nges pas 'khri ba bcad/ 'jig rten bya byed rgyab tu bsgyur/ 'khor ba'i las la zhen pa zlog/ rigs drug 'khor ba'i sdug bsngal yang / rang gi steng du yong nges 
2a3(ta): pas/ rgyud la bsam zhing nges shes bskyed/ rigs drug pa ma bu gnyen la/ bdag phyogs med pa'i snying rje bskyed/ le lo'i dgra gnom brtson 'grus nya la bskyen/ dad 
2a4(ta): pa'i stobs bskyed thar pa'i lam la 'jug/ gnyis pa nang gizhes pa sbyang pa ni/ byang chub mchog tu sems bskyed de/ m rig 'khrul pa'i sems can la/ snying je / 
2a5(ta): byams dga' btang snyoms sogs/ tshad med snying rje bzhi ldan sgom/ phyi nang gsang gsum yang gsang gi/ skyabs gnas bla ma bder gzhegs la/ rtse gcig gdung bas 
2b1(ta): skyabs su 'gro/ nyon mongs sdig greb sbyang ba'i phyir/ b'ode nams tshigs ni bsgags par bya/ rab kyis 'khor gsum song dag bya/ 'bring gis tshigs mchod rgya chen gyis/ bder / 
2b2(ta): ghegs mkha' 'gro bon sbyong mtchod/ bar tshad na ba'i gsol ba gdab/ dpon gsas bla ma mnyes par bya/ tha ma mthral rnam pa bani/ dus gsum dus bzher 'brul bar bya/ 
2b3(ta): sgrib pa sbyang ba'i rim pa ni/ mchod byin lan chags gtor ma yis/ rigs drug lan chags sdig srib sbyang / tsha ba chab gtor nye 'don dang / phyag bskor bya zhing lus srib sbyang / 
2b4(ta): skyabs 'gro snying po bzla brjod kyis/ ngag gi sgrib pa sbyang bar bya/ kun bzang thugs rje'i 'od zer gyis/ rigs drug dug lnga'i sa bon bcom/ a dkar 'od zer 'phro 'du yis/ dug 
2b5(ta): lnga yid kyi sgrib pa sbyang / de lhar sngon 'gro s+dzogs pa dang / mtshan ma'i s+dzas la sems bzung ste/ sku gsung thugs kyi mtshan ma gsum/ sku ni lus tshad tchen gang pa/ dmigs pa / 
2b6(ta): rim gyis yos la gtad/ g.yung drung ya dkar gsal la dod/ 'doms gang gang bde'i thad du bzhag/ lus ni mnyam bzhag lnga ldan bca'/ lus kyi gnad drug dbang po'i gnad lnga 
3a1(ta): bstan/ skyil klung bca' b rkang pa'i gnad dang gcig/ mda' sdug ltar bsrang pa tshigs pa'i gnad dang gnyis/ snyid dpang bstod pa rkad pa'i gnad dang gsum/ lag pa / 
3a2(ta): gnyis yar bteg ste/ ro stod sang sr gseng ba byang khog gi gnad dang bzhi/ phyag mnyam par bzhag pa lag pa'i gnad dang lnga/ mgrin pa lcags k+ya ltar bkug pa ske 'jzing gi 
3a3(ta): gnad dang drug go/ ldzags ya rkan la ma rig pa le'i gnad dang gcig/ spyan kyi s+dje ma ma sprad pa mig gi gnad dang gnyis/ shangs lag blung 'phra la snyoms par bya ba sna'i gnad dang 
3a4(ta): gsum/ snyan sgra phyir mi 'breng ba rna ba'i gnad dang bzhi/ kha so rang lugs su bzhag pa so dang mtshu'i gnad dang lnga'o// ngag ni smra brjod bral bar bya/ yid ni dus gsum yengs med / 
3a5(ta): du/ rjes mi gcod cing sngon ma bsu/ da lha nyid du bsam mi bya/ the tshom med par drag tu gtad/ rtog med g.yo mad yings med du/ cang lhod med par preng re gtad/ thun tshad 
3a6(ta): khams kyi tshed dang sbyar/ cung zhig goms par gyur pa na/ ched du sgrim yang mi dgos te/ ngna la cung zad gnas pa dang / sems ni zin rtags sna tshogs 'byung / de dus god cing khad 
3b1(ta): kyis khrid/ sems kyi bzung thabs bstan pa'o// gnas lugs don gyi lta ba la/ mtshan med don la bzhag thabs rnam pa gsum/ reg pa gzhan du mi g.yo bar bya ste/ bya ci / 
3b2(ta): ba tshang du 'dzul ba ltar bzhag/ bya rtsol dang bral ba skyes bu bya ba zin pa ltar bzhag/ ma bcos lhug pa bu chung cig la bzhag pa ltar bzhag/ dpe ni gar spyin sbang chags / 
3b3(ta): 'ra/ rten ni gang zag rnam gsum la/ blo dang 'tshams pa'i ngo sprod bstan/ bying rhugs skyon gyi bcos thabs ni/ rig pa gzengs bstod par yang bskyed/ mtho sar sgom zhing mkha' 
3b4(ta): la gtad/ so la dar phyar bzhin du bcos/ rnam rtog 'phro rgod mang ba la/ rus sbal mkhar gzhing bzhag ltar bcos/ khyim stong rkun mo zhugs ltar bcos/ dug la sman gyis 
3b5(ta): bsgyur lthar bcos/ dpehi byi bo gar ma'i bzo/ ma bcos pa ni bcos pa'i mchog/ sems kyi btsa' thabs bstan pa ni/ rgyal po' btsun mo lta bur btsa'/ dmu rgod ta 
3b6(ta): 'dul bzhin du btsa'/ yid bzhin nor bu bzhin du btsa'/ shes bzhin bya ras sod bar bya/ de ni sems kyi btsa' thabs so// ngang pa'i rgyal po chu 'byed bzhin/ sems nyid ngang du 
4a1(ta): / y/ gdar na bcad/ sgag mos me long lta ba dang / shel sgong byi dor byas pa bzhin/ sems nyid gng du gdar sha bcad/ bcad pas bon sems gcig tu rtogs/ spyed pa rang 
4a2(ta): shar thugs 'byung nga nyid du/ gyad kyis gzhu bdung rgyud bzhin du/ thang lhod med par spyod pa ni/ dpe ni chu la nya 'phyo 'nra/ 'bras ba tsan dan lo 'bras 'dra/ gser gling pbyin pa ni 
4a3(ta): bzhin no/ lhun grub r dg bral ba yin/ dge 'd 'byung ba'i zhir ba sin/ dponi mkha' la nyi shar 'dra/ ddus gang chad 'di lta 'byang / tcig rtugs med pa tsig dpal/ 
4a4(ta): nyon mongs zel gnon seng ge 'dra/ nyams nga med pa khyung ldeng 'dra/ gsal la dangs pa nam mkha' dp/ drid tshad rtags ni 'di ltar 'byung / lus ni yang bzshing bal 'dra/ dbugs 
4a5(ta): ne rgyu ba m tshor nhing / nyams dga' khams bdi rieg pa gag la/ me g.som 'gyur re rgyal la/ gun kyung shron me btegs pa bzhin/ gsal la khrib gsogs med pa 'byung / 
4a6(ta): rgya mtsho lta bur kha gting med/ nam mkhar mdung bskor yangs dog med/ lhang lhan nor gnas pa dang / nyams gyi snang ba sna tshogs 'char/ lhag mthong rig pa ngo sprod pas/ ban 
4b1(ta): nyid ngang du sems nyid grol/ lhun grub lta bas thag bcad de/ 'ubs chub chen por la zla'o// de ltar rtogs pa'i gang zag la/ lus sems bim rig bral ba'i tshe/ sems ni skye 
4b2(ta): med rangs zen/ snang ba sku gsum rtsal du shar/ dug lnga ye zhes lnga ru grol/ nyon mongs sangs nas ye shes rgyas/ khyung dang sang gi' bu bzhin du / lus rgya zhig nas mngon sangs 
4b3(ta): rgyas/ rtogs pa mngon gyur sangs rgyas so// zhes gsungs so// sa ma ya/ kun tu bzang po rang rig mnyam nyid ngang la phyag 'tshal lo// rigs kyi bu gdang dang mi ldan ma rtogs / 
4b4(ta): blo zhan rnams/ nges par 'dres zhing yongs su grol bya'i phyir/ gzhi nas bslab pa man ngag zab mo'i don/ bder gshegs dgongs rgyud dgu'i thugs kyi bcud/ nyi shu rtsa bzhi nyams 
4b5(ta): kyi man ngag bshad/ skal ldan blo' 'ben la thog par shig/ sa ma sa/ snang srid 'khor 'das bon rnams kun/ thams cad byang chub sems su s+dzogs/ ye nas sems nyid 
4b6(ta): mnyam par gnas/ rang 'byung ye shes rang gsal yin/ dngos dang rnam pa snang ba rnams/ rig pa phyi nang zang thal yin/ gsal la ma sgrib tsig mtha' med/ ma bcos ma bslud 
5a1(ta): ste nyid la/ gngala bsreg cha ma 'gags pa/ gsal sting nam mkha'i rang bzhin can/ mbtha' dbyung med pa'i bde chen po/ con nyid bde chen kling yang ste/ 
5a2(ta): sems nyid stong pa'i ye zhes ni/ rgyu yis ma bskyed rang 'byung yin/ rkyen gyis ma bsud zang bal yin/ byed pas ma bcos se ma yin/ ye nas gnas pas lhug pa yin/ bstan 
5a3(ta): du med pas skye med yin/ 'di don rang sems rig pa 'di/ gzhan du mi btsal rang la gsal/ thog mtha' mi gnas 'du 'bral med/ kun gyis mi rig cig le che/ zhes gsungs 
5a4(ta): so// sa ma ya/ de'i ngang la bzhag pa'i thabs/ gzhan du mi btsal rang la btsal/ sgom med ngang las yengs med du / lus ni khong glod bag yangs su/ shes pa rang mdngs so mar / 
5a5(ta): bnag/ dbugs ni 'phra rang snyoms par dbyung / shes pa mi hrab ma bsdam zhing / ma bsdu mi gnan rang babs du/ gyi na so ma thug par bhag/ can sku bde ba chen po la/ 
5a6(ta): yul du mi bzung brten mi bca'/ ched du gang yang mi bsgrub cing / shugs 'char gang yang dgag mi bya/ don du ci yang mi gnyer la/ rtsol bas nan gyis ched mi gtad/ gsal / 
5b1(ta): la rtog pa med bzhin du/ mi rtog ma bca' rang lugs bnag/ yul gyi skye mched sna tshigs dang / yang yang 'khrul pa'i nyon mongs la/ 'dzin sems nang nas ma bca' zhing / 
5b2(ta): bzung yul phyi nas mi bkag gi/ skyon yon gnyis su ma lha zhing / dgag sgrub med pa'i na la bzhag/ rang bzhin ma bcos de nyid la/ rang gsal chen po rang la 'char/ 
5b3(ta): 'khrul pa'i nyon mongs rnam rtog gi/ mtshan ma sna tshogs ci byung yang / dgag yang mi bya rjes mi 'jug/ mi chags rang bzhin rang yal bzhag/ ngo bo ban nyid rang gsal ba'o// 
5b4(ta): sa ma sa/ de ltar mnyam par bzhag pa'i tshe/ 'phro rgod dang ni bying rgugs dang / skyon gyi rnam pa gnyis byung na/ 'phro rgod skyon gyi bcos thabs ni/ shes pa na rgod srab yan 
5b5(ta): bzhin/ yul la skye mched 'phro rgod cing / rnam rtog tha dad skye 'gyur na/ ched du ma bkag mi blang zhing / mi bsu rjes su mi 'breng bar/ 'phro rgod btang la so mar 'dug/ shes 
5b6(ta): bzhin yid kyi bya ra btang / ji ltar mched pa bde chen dbyings/ bzhag pas rang log rang zhir 'ong / de ni 'phro rgod bcos thabs so// bying rgugs skyon gyi bcos thabs ni/ dmu long 
6a1(ta): yu/ rgya mtshor byeng ba bzhin/ shes pa'i tshigs drug mun 'theb cing / rugs shing byeng bar gyur pa ni/ phyi 'gags nang 'dus mthong thos med/ yid la sdug pos zhin pa / 
6a2(ta): bzhin/ de la zhes pa khong glod la/ dpang dang gzangs bstod bag yangs kyi/ ngna la zhes pa 'dzin med par/ rang bzhin rtog med yi 'byams su/ yi khyab chen por gtang ba ni/ 
6a3(ta): skyon rnams rang zhi rang grol nas/ ye shes 'od gsal chen po'o// zhes gsungs so// sa ma ya/ de ltar snang ba'i ye shes nyid/ 'dzin rtig bral ba'i g.yung rung ste/ gnyis med bde 
6a4(ta): chen rang la 'char/ de ltar gnas pa'i man ngag ni/ ma rig rig par bya ba yi/ bon ni gud na ye nas med/ ma bcos pa ni bon nyid la/ ma sgrib pa ni sems nyid kyis/ ma 
6a5(ta): yeangs pa'i ting 'dzin ni/ ma g.yos pa'i nga du sgom/ de ltar gnas pa'i nga nyid la/ rig shes gsal ba rang la 'char/ des na bon sems thams cad kun/ snying po byang chub sems 
6a6(ta): nyid du/ bon sku bde ba chen po nyid/ nyams su myong zhing gsal bar 'gyur/ de yang bon sku ji ltar na/ dngos po gang yang ma yin pa/ ji lta bur yang brjod ma btub/ gang lta bur 
6b1(ta): yang gdags mi brlab/ ddon nyams su myong par 'gyur/ zhes gsungs'o// sams/ de lta ba'i bon nyid la/ dngos po'i ngokhbo m grub p/ dbyebs dang ba dog bzun du bed/ de / 
6b2(ta): med dngos po las 'das pa/ 'di zhes bya bar bstan byar med/ rgyu dang gzhi' rtyen med pas/ skye shi' rgyun rnams ye nas chad/ gzhi dang rtsa ba med pa yis/ rag ni gar yang lus 
6b3(ta): ma myong / thig ma tha ma'i dus med pas/ 'du 'bral med pa'i khyab bdal che/ mtha' dang dbus zhes ma grub pas/ rig pa'i 'od gsal khyab par gtang / de ltar gsal ba'i man 
6b4(ta): ngag gis/ bon sems ma lus gdar na bcad/ de ni dgongs pa'i zhe shugs yin/ de ltar gdar sha bcad pa yis/ nyon mongs thams cad ye shes su/ zhen pa rang log sdug bsngal 
6b5(ta): sangs/ 'dzin rtog thams cad kho thag chod/ snang ba thams cad bde chen gyi/ byang chub sems su ye gsal phyir/ the tshom sgro 'dogs gdar sha chod/ rnam rtog thams cad ma 
6b6(ta): bcos pa'i/ bon sems gnyis su ma bcad pas/ spros pa thams cad gting nas dag/ skyon dang yon tan dgag sgrub bral/ snying po theg ler la bcad pas/ bying rgod gol sgrib 
7a1(ta): thams cad zlig/ theg pa dgu'i thob bya kun/ de las 'byung bar la bcad pas/ dman pa'i 'bras bu kho tag tshod/ ces gsungs so// sa ma sa/ de tshe gsang ba'i / 
7a2(ta): spyod pa ni/ lha sgom 'brel ba'i nga nyid du/ 'gro nyal 'dug sdod spyod yul du/ sgo gsum gang lhar spyad kyang snying po ya/ de'i don las 'da' mi srid/ dper na nya'i gang 'phyos kyang / 
7a3(ta): tchu'i nag las 'da' mi sred/ de bzhin sgo gsum gang ltar du/ spyod kyang bde chen snying po'i ngang / dman pa'i las rnams gang spyod kyang / skyon yon gang gis rig mi chus/ bzang ngan 
7a4(ta): spyod pa ma lus kyang / bde chen snying po'i spyod pa las/ ye nas ma 'das lhun grub pas/ blang dang dor ba ye med phyir/ kun tu bzang po'i spyod pa'o// de lta bu ru rtogs pa'i tshe
7a5(ta): gol s rdul tsam mi 'byung pas/ rgyud dag rtogs pa mngon gyur gyi/ sangs rgyas yin zhesngas bshad do// sa ma ya/ don nyid ye s+dzogs cig le che/ de la 'bras bu brtar 
7a6(ta): btags nas/ rang gi sems nyid bde chen las/ ma gtogs 'bras bu gzhan mi tshol/ sems nyid bon sku gnyug ma de/ rang grol chen por gnas pa'i phyir/ bon rnams ma 
7b1(ta): bcos rang sm/ bnag pa nyid kyis lhan gyis s+dzogs/ ma bsdung gcig ta dril ba/ m pros ye gdal chen por khyab/ rtsol sgrub bral ba'i 'bras ba d/ 'bad pas gzhan / 
7b2(ta): 'byung cang ma yin/ rang gi rig pa ma 'khrul bar/ mthar byin mngon du gyur nas kyang / tshad du s+dzogs nas klong du gyur/ rang dbang thob nas lhun gyis grub/ thag chod rtsol sgrub 
7b3(ta): gdang du gyur/ 'bras bu zhes su tha snyad btags/ de ltar gnas pa'i dgongs pa yis/ dus gsum mnyam pa'i ngag nyid las/ shugs kyis snang ba'i yon tan ni/ rtags dang rang nyams 
7b4(ta): drid tshad dang / rnam gsum las sogs 'byung ba kun/ gsum po skabs kyi cha nyid du / 'byung dang mi 'byung khyad par med/ 'byung yang 'dzin 'khrul 'gag pa med/ ma byung bsgrub dang 
7b5(ta): dga' brod med/ gang la 'gal ba med pa la/ 'gal bar bzung na de nyid gol/ ma byung gdang gyur shin tu mchog/ byung yang rtog med gnyis kyi cha/ de ni mi rtog mi g.yo ba'i/ 
7b6(ta): bsam gtan ngang la rgyun du gnas/ zhes gsungs so// sa ma ya/ 'chi med sems kyi ngo bo la/ skye shi gdod nas ye med kyang / res shig lus bor shes pa de/ lus sems 
8a1(ta): bral ba'i dus nyid du/ se mtshams bar rde sna dus de/ yid ni 'di du rgyu ds dang / spyod pul gzugs brnyan mtsha dus te/ pyi blung rnams yongs du 'gags/ sgra 
8a2(ta): nyid nang du 'dus pa'i dus/ snang ba 'di lngar shar ba'i dus/ rig pa zer du 'phro ba'i dus/ gdes pa'i lus dang rig pa' bung / bral bas bskal pa du ma'i yun/ rang snang 'khrul pas sdug 
8a3(ta): bsngal shyong / rang sems nyid du ngospd pas/ bon nyid ma bcos gtug mar shar/ de yang ji ltar 'char zhe na/ sngon sgrib bral nas rig pa gsal/ je bzhin gnas pa'i snying po de/ 
8a4(ta): rang sems rig pa dmar thag bcad/ snang stong bcas pa'i bon rnams kun/ 'dzin rtog snyems chags dag dang bral/ gdod nas dus gsum rgyu med pa'i/ rang 'byung skye med gnas pa 
8a5(ta): de/ rig pas sems nyid mngon du gyur/ de yang snga ma'i man ngag gis/ mtshams sbyar gyis ni d byung ste/ mthong ba'i yul med gar gsal ba/ gsal yang 'di zhes dngos zhen med/ 
8a6(ta): rang so gnyug mar gnas pa de/ lhang nge lhan ner gsal bar 'gyur/ skad cig de la mtshams sbyar bas/ bar dor yon tan lhun grub pa/ rang 'byung thig le'i ngang du grol/ sprin med 
8b1(ta): mkha' la nyi shar 'dra/ rtogs pa mngon gyur sangs rgyas de/ bde ba chen po'i ngang la gnas/ tshegs med don chi'i man ngag 'di/ 'chi kha ma'i skyes bu'am/ skal ldan snod ldan 
8b2(ta): gshen rab ni/ gs thub gting zab nyams len mkhas/ de lta bu la bstan par bya/ snod med gcsam bu kha khyer mkhan/ don la 'chal bas nyams len med/ de lta bu la 
8b3(ta): shin tu gsang / sgra tshig tsam yang brjod mi bya/ zhes so// sa mas/ rigs kyi bu bder ghegs dgongs rgyud dgu'i thuags kyi bcud/ nye shu rtsa bzhi nyams kyi bman gag drel/ la 
8b4(ta): sgom gnad kyi gzer bu mnyam bzhag sgom pa'i man ngag 'di/ skal ldan ma nor lam la 'khrid phyir bstan/ yang gs thugs kyi dkyil du zhog/ skal med rnams la zhin tu 
8b5(ta): gsang / dus mthar mi nub 'gro don byed par shog/ sa ma ya/ zhes sprul pa'i sku yis gyir spungs chen po la gsungs so// mtshan med la sems bzung zhing / mnyam par 
8b6(ta): bzhag pa'i man ngag rig 'dzin gyi snyan rgyud/ mi tshig gi lhad mazhugs pa'i gdams pa/ snyan rgyud yig ger bskod pa/ sa magsa/ rgya rgya rgya/ yab// 
1a1(tha): yg// dges rhyad dgo' chig lang bthagsso// // kun tu bzang po thugs rje rgyun chad med la phyag 'tsal lo// ton nyid kyab bdal dbyings kyi 'og min na/ ye nyid 
1a2(tha): ston pa brjod med bon sku yis/ rang 'byung ka dag skye med nang nyid nas/ thugs rje'i ston pa'i thugs kyi dkyil du bshad/ ye nas brjod du med pa'i don du dgongs/ mi g.yo khyab 
1a3(tha): bdal dbyings kyi 'og min na/ thugs rje'i ston pa kun tu bzang po yis/ thugs nyid g.yo ba med pa'i ngng nyid nas/ sprul pa'i ston pa'i thugs kyi dkyil du bshad/ kun khyab nam 
1a4(tha): mkha' lta bu'i don du dgongs/ lhun grub khyab bdal dbyings kyi 'og min na/ ma g.yos ngang las g.yo ba'i cho 'phrul gyis/ bon gyi sku la mtshan dpe yongs su s+dzogs/ gang la 
1a5(tha): gang 'dul gang mos sku ru bstan/ sprul pa'i ston pa gnhen lha 'di dkar gyis/ thugs rje chen po'i byen rlabs nga nyid nas/ zer yang spul sku'i thugs kyi dkyil du bshad/ mtha' 
1a6(tha): dbus med pa 'od kyi snying po can/ mkha' la nyi shar lta bu'i don du dgongs/ bar lha 'd gsal lha'i 'og min na/ rig pa'i ston pa tshad med 'di ldan gyis/ ye zhes rang shar chen 
1b1(tha): po'i ngang nyid nas/ 'phrul ghen snang ldan thugs kyi dkyil du bshad/ nyi 'di nyi zer lta bu'i don du dgongs/ mgon btsun pya yul gser steng 'og min na/ thabs chen ston pa / 
1b2(tha): 'dhrul ghen snang ldan gyis/ rang rig rang gsal sgrib med ngng nyid nas/ bar snang ston pa'i thugs kyi dkyil du bshad/ chu dang chu zla lta bu'i don du dgongs/ sum hu rtsa gsum lha'i 
1b3(tha): 'og min na/ bar snang khu byug spul pa'i ston pa yis/ thabs shes dbyer med rol pa'i ngng nyid nas/ gsang ba'i yum gyi thugs kyi dkyil du bshad/ snang la rang bzhin med pa'i 
1b4(tha): don du dgongs/ rin chen g.su steng tshal gyi 'og min na/ bzang za ring btsun shes rab yum nyid kyis/ dbyings zhes dbyer med stong pa'i ngag nyid nas/ 'chi med gtsug pud thugs 
1b5(tha): kyi dkyil du bshad/ gsal stong dbye ba med pa'i don dudgongs/ gsu lung zhel sdug gsang ba'i 'og min na/ mkha' dbyings spul pa'i ston pa 'cho med gtsug pud kyis/ dgongs 
1b6(tha): pa'i rnying khu phrul du phyin pa 'di/ rgyud lung man ngag tshig don 'brel ba ru/ rgyud khungs ston pa'i thugs kyi dkyil du bshad/ gsang ba'i man ngag don du 'dus par dgongs/ lha yul
